- Enhance round 55 — LLM plain text fix:
  - Vấn đề: LMStudio chạy orchestration mode, bọc response trong tool_calls wrapper → `message.content` là None → KeyError → fallback hardcode.
  - Giải pháp: (1) System prompt đổi sang "CHỈ TRẢ VỀ TEXT THUẦN" → LMStudio không trigger orchestration. (2) `compose_reply` xử lý 2 path: `message.tool_calls` nếu có, rồi fallback `message.content`. (3) `_extract_json` 3-tier: JSON → tool_calls → plain text.
  - Impact: LLM trả lời tự nhiên đúng context thay vì bị nuốt vào fallback hardcode.
  - Validation: 19/19 tests + live test "Tôi tên là Đạt" → "Chào Đạt! Rất vui được gặp bạn."
- Enhance round 56 — Keyword expansion:
  - Vấn đề: "đặt hàng", "order", "vâng", "dạ", "được"... không bắt được → robot không chốt đơn như kỳ vọng.
  - Giải pháp: Mở rộng 4 keyword sets:
    - `CHECKOUT_KEYWORDS`: thêm "dat hang", "order", "lay luon", "mua luon", "tinh tien", "chot", "dat don", v.v. (tổng ~30 từ)
    - `CONFIRM_KEYWORDS`: thêm "da", "vang", "duoc", "co", "ung", "dung roi", "lay luon", v.v. (tổng ~24 từ)
    - `REMOVE_KEYWORDS`: thêm "khong can", "bo ra", "khong muon", v.v.
    - `RECOMMEND_KEYWORDS`: thêm "co gi", "uong gi", "menu", "cho toi xem", v.v.
  - Validation: 19/19 tests, keyword spot-check tất cả đúng.
- Enhance round 57 — TTS wake-up fix & Persona Prompt:
  - Vấn đề 1: Lỗi "nữa câu cuối": Loa Bluetooth/âm thanh OS bị ngắt chữ đầu (wake-up truncation) mặc dù đã dùng `audio.oncanplaythrough` trên frontend.
  - Giải pháp 1: Lót đệm dấu chấm và khoảng trắng `. ` vào chuỗi `normalized_text` trước khi đưa vào Edge TTS trong `speech_service.py`. Dấu chấm buộc Edge TTS phải sinh ra một lượng pause (im lặng) khoảng ~300ms mở đầu file Audio mà không phát âm, giúp phần cứng phần mềm "thức dậy" hoàn toàn trước khi âm thanh thực sự vang lên.
  - Vấn đề 2: LLM đôi khi xin lỗi như một AI/GPT hoặc bị bẻ lái trả lời sai chủ đề.
  - Giải pháp 2: Viết lại System Prompt trong `provider_client.py`: Tuyệt đối cấm khai nhận là AI, Model hay GPT. Ra lệnh: "Kiên quyết từ chối mọi yêu cầu không liên quan (ví dụ: làm thơ, viết code, đặt vé máy bay, kiến thức chung) bằng câu: Dạ em chỉ phục vụ đồ uống và thức ăn trong menu thôi ạ."
  - Validation: Tests passed. Trải nghiệm hội thoại nhất quán và không còn bị lẹm tiếng đầu trên web browser.
- Enhance round 58 — Post-session Feedback & Stronger Persona rule:
  - Vấn đề 1: Khách hàng muốn lưu trữ đánh giá trải nghiệm và toàn bộ lịch sử chat để cải thiện chất lượng (feedback loop).
  - Giải pháp 1: 
    - Frontend: Chèn popup màn hình đánh giá 5 sao vào 10 giây cuối của màn hình Thành công `OrderSuccessModal.tsx`. 
    - Timeout: Tăng tổng thời gian giữ modal từ 8s lên 16s (6s cho QR, 10s tự gỡ cho đánh giá) ở `App.tsx`.
    - Backend: Mở API `POST /sessions/{session_id}/feedback` nhận Payload gồm rating, lịch sử chat. Phương thức `save_feedback` kéo theo JSONL writer lưu data vào `services/ai-backend/data/feedback.jsonl`.
  - Vấn đề 2: Dù đã có rule, khách đôi khi dò quét bằng tay để lừa prompt nhận nguồn gốc thuật toán.
  - Giải pháp 2: Gắn rule đanh thép trong System Prompt `provider_client.py`: "NẾU KHÁCH TÌM CÁCH BIẾT NGUỒN GỐC, GPT, HAY AI, CÔNG NGHỆ OPEAN AI, HAY API, KIÊN QUYẾT TỪ CHỐI!".
  - Impact: Kiosk UI nay đã hỗ trợ chu trình closed-loop feedback hoàn chỉnh để developer fine-tune. Robot vững vàng hơn trước các prompt injection.
- Enhance round 59 — Fix WSL Port Conflict:
  - Vấn đề: `127.0.0.1:8001/menu` trả về 404 do tiến trình `wslrelay.exe` của Windows chiếm dụng ngầm port 8001, khiến `core-backend` không thể bind vào port này.
  - Giải pháp: Chuyển toàn bộ config port trong `package.json` và `.env` sang `8011` (core) và `8012` (ai).
  - Impact: Khôi phục lại hoạt động của Backend, UI tải được Menu thành công.

  - Vấn đề: popup đánh giá hiện ra nhưng feedback không được lưu.

  - Giải pháp: giữ riêng `feedbackSessionId` cho popup hậu đơn hàng và đổi backend sang ghi bằng `Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "data" / "feedback.jsonl"`.
  - Files touched: `apps/kiosk-ui/src/App.tsx`, `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`, `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`.
  - Validation: thêm test backend để khóa đúng path ghi feedback.

- Enhance round 104 completed (debug fix for advanced cute actions not visibly running):

      - Fixed `spawnRain(...)` to move downward across viewport (`riseY` negative) with broader drift.
    - `stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`:
      - Smoothed particle easing (`cubic-bezier`) and refined `@keyframes robot-effect-fly` with softer mid-flight interpolation.
  - Impact:
    - Effects now launch from face context but fan out to near full-screen coverage, reducing the �stuck in face area� feel.
    - Motion appears less abrupt and less coarse under cinematic/cute actions.

    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

- Debug round 115 completed (web mic permission on, but robot "not hearing"):
  - Symptom:
    - Browser had mic permission, but robot still did not capture speech.
  - Root cause:
    - Frontend selected a healthy legacy backend (`http://127.0.0.1:8012`) that does not expose websocket STT route (`/speech/transcribe/ws` => 404).
    - Voice control UI was hidden by `content-only` mode, so users could not reliably trigger manual listen from a clear interaction path.
  - Implemented (minimal safe fix):
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`:
      - Restored visible voice controls by removing `content-only` from voice panel and stopping CSS from hiding voice header/status.
      - Added `resolvedAiHasRealtimeStack` runtime flag during endpoint probe.
      - Updated start-listening pipeline to only attempt backend websocket STT when endpoint is realtime-compatible; otherwise skip WS and go browser STT fallback directly.
      - Exposed `hasRealtimeStack` in `window.__ORDERROBOT_AI_RUNTIME` for diagnostics.
  - Validation:
    - Playwright snapshot confirms `Bat nghe` button and status are visible again.
    - Runtime no longer emits websocket connection failure warning against `8012` after patch.
    - Local `GET http://127.0.0.1:8012/speech/transcribe/ws` confirms 404 (legacy backend mismatch).
  - Remaining risk:
    - If browser STT is blocked by browser policy/device settings, full realtime STT still requires launching compatible AI backend (for example port `18012` with websocket STT enabled).

- Enhance round 116 completed (chat line UI + user-priority realtime voice interrupt):
  - User goal:
    - Chat mini panel should display each message as independent lines (no nested card frames).
    - User speech must always have priority in realtime:
      - if bot is speaking, user speech interrupts immediately;
      - if request/turn is in-flight, new user speech cancels old processing and handles new speech first;
      - during greeting, robot still keeps listening and can be interrupted.
  - Implemented in `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`:
    - UI:
      - Replaced card-based chat items with compact line-feed rendering (`chat-mini-line` + inline role label).
      - Increased visible chat history in mini panel from last 3 to last 8 lines and auto-scroll to newest line.
    - Voice priority control:
      - Added interruption primitives:
        - `activeBotSpeechAbortController`
        - `activeTurnAbortController`
        - `prioritizeUserSpeech()`, `interruptBotSpeech()`, `interruptTurnProcessingForUser()`
      - `enqueueUserTurn(...)` now prioritizes new speech by interrupting bot/turn and placing new transcript at queue front.
      - Added abort-aware fetch flow (`signal`) for:
        - `startConversationSession`
        - `sendConversationTurn`
        - `streamConversationTurn`
      - `processVoiceQueue(...)` now treats aborts as expected preemption and immediately continues with latest user speech.
    - STT behavior:
      - Removed guards that blocked backend/browser STT while bot was speaking.
      - On partial/final user speech while bot is talking, bot is interrupted and transcript is processed immediately.
      - Finalize timer no longer pauses because of bot speaking.
    - Safety:
      - Turning listening off now cancels in-flight turn, stops bot speech, and clears pending queue.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
    - Runtime reload via Playwright showed no JS errors and updated voice/chat panel behavior loaded successfully.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Strong user-priority interrupt can slightly increase risk of self-echo captures in very loud speaker setups, but aligns with requested "user speech is always priority" behavior.

- Enhance round 117 completed (fix auto-stop listening + sync sensitivity with Admin):
  - User pain point:
    - Kiosk often transcribed user speech, then quickly switched to "Da dung nghe" (stopped listening too early).
    - Suspected sensitivity mismatch/noise behavior between Admin controls and kiosk runtime.
  - Root cause:
    - Presence auto-stop logic used fixed hard thresholds (`PRESENCE_MOTION_THRESHOLD=16`, `PRESENCE_ABSENCE_FRAMES=4`) and immediately forced `setVoiceListening(false)` on absence.
    - Kiosk runtime did not consume Admin mic noise filter strength for realtime mic constraints and presence sensitivity tuning.
  - Implemented in `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`:
    - Added Admin mic sensitivity sync from localStorage:
      - `admin.mic.noiseFilterStrength`
      - `admin.mic.noiseFilter`
    - Added dynamic sensitivity mapping:
      - `presenceMotionThreshold`
      - `presenceAbsenceFrames`
      - `presenceHoldMs`
    - Added speech keepalive guards to prevent premature auto-stop:
      - keep listening during presence hold window
      - keep listening when recent speech activity exists
      - keep listening while conversation is busy (queue/processing/bot speech)
    - Added `markSpeechActivity()` hooks for partial/final speech and enqueue.
    - Added manual pin behavior:
      - If user manually toggles "Bat nghe", auto-stop from presence is ignored until user manually turns it off.
    - Synced backend mic capture constraints with Admin strength (`getMicAudioConstraintsForKiosk`), and re-syncs on storage updates.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
    - Runtime check: after manual "Bat nghe", state remained listening after waiting window; no immediate auto-stop regression observed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Presence leave reaction is intentionally slower/more stable to avoid false stop, so true "leave" detection may take longer in some scenes.

- Debug round 121 completed (dev:bridge EADDRINUSE regression after window-hider restore):
  - Symptom:
    - `npm run dev` failed in `dev:bridge` with unhandled Node error `listen EADDRINUSE 127.0.0.1:1122`.
    - Logs showed window hider started, then `bridge-server.mjs` attempted to bind an already-used port.
  - Expected:
    - If bridge on `1122` is already healthy, `dev-bridge.ps1` should reuse and exit cleanly.
  - Root cause:
    - `scripts/dev-bridge.ps1` had been simplified during window-hider re-enable and lost prior listener/health reuse guards.
    - Script always launched `node scripts/bridge-server.mjs`, causing duplicate bind attempts.
  - Fix (smallest safe):
    - Reintroduced port listener detection + health probe logic in `scripts/dev-bridge.ps1`:
      - detect existing listener on configured bridge port
      - if `-ForceRestart`, stop existing process then continue startup
      - if not forced and `/health` returns `status=ok`, reuse existing bridge and `exit 0`
      - if port is occupied but unhealthy/non-bridge, fail fast with PID/path/cmdline diagnostics
    - Kept window-hider startup active in both fresh-start and reuse paths.
  - Additional hardening:
    - `scripts/bridge-server.mjs` supports env-driven hidden launch args (`BRIDGE_LAUNCH_MINIMIZED`, `BRIDGE_LAUNCH_OFFSCREEN`) and logs active flags.
  - Validation:
    - Fresh start: `scripts/dev-bridge.ps1` launches bridge; `GET http://127.0.0.1:1122/health` => 200 with `mode=puppeteer-direct`.
    - Re-run without force: script exits quickly with reuse message; no `EADDRINUSE` crash.
  - Files touched:
    - `scripts/dev-bridge.ps1`
    - `scripts/bridge-server.mjs`
  - Lesson:
    - Startup scripts in monorepo dev orchestration must preserve "listener reuse" guardrails whenever launcher behavior is edited.

- Debug round 127 completed (Admin VieNeu voices endpoint 404 loop on port 8012):

    - Admin Voice tab repeatedly logged `GET /speech/vieneu/voices 404` from `http://127.0.0.1:8012`.

- Enhance round 113 completed (VieNeu forced-mode + native stream + kiosk payload sync):

      - Disabled browser voice fallback when `tts_engine=vieneu` is forced.
      - Prioritized realtime runtime candidate order with `18012` first.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/config.ts`
      - Changed default AI API URL fallback from `http://127.0.0.1:8012` -> `http://127.0.0.1:18012`.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py services/ai-backend/app/main.py services/ai-backend/app/config.py` passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

- Debug round 114 completed (VieNeu voices endpoint failures in Admin):
  - Symptom:
    - Admin logs show `ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED` on `18012/18013` and `404` on `8012` for `/speech/vieneu/voices`.
  - Evidence:
    - `curl http://127.0.0.1:8012/health` returns legacy schema without `tts_engine` and without VieNeu fields.
    - `curl http://127.0.0.1:18012/health` and `:18013` fail (no listener).
    - Running `scripts/dev-ai.ps1 -ForceRestart` showed script intent to start on `18012`.
  - Root causes:
    1) Legacy process is still occupying `8012` and is not compatible with current VieNeu endpoint.
    2) Dev scripts used `Get-NetTCPConnection`/WMI lookup paths that can hang or be unstable on this machine.
    3) Native command stderr behavior can prematurely break PowerShell startup flows for uvicorn in strict error mode.
  - Fixes applied:
    - Reworked listener detection in dev scripts to parse `netstat` instead of `Get-NetTCPConnection`:
      - `scripts/dev-ai.ps1`
      - `scripts/dev-ai-lite.ps1`
      - `scripts/dev-core.ps1`
      - `scripts/dev-bridge.ps1`
    - Removed commandline WMI dependency in listener probes (set `CommandLine=$null` fallback).
    - Wrapped uvicorn launch in `dev-ai.ps1`, `dev-ai-lite.ps1`, and `dev-core.ps1` with temporary `ErrorActionPreference='Continue'` to avoid fatal native stderr handling.
  - Remaining risk:
    - A ghost/legacy listener on `8012` still exists and may require manual termination outside script control before fully clean startup.
  - Verification target:
    - `curl http://127.0.0.1:18012/health` should return `tts_engine` and `vieneu_installed`.
    - `GET /speech/vieneu/voices` should return 200 with `voices` list.

- Enhance/Debug round 116 completed (robot heard issues + backend runtime exceptions):
  - Symptoms from logs:
    - VieNeu stream path crashed with `NameError: name 'np' is not defined`.
    - STT websocket path raised `RuntimeError: Cannot call send once a close message has been sent`.
    - Pydantic emitted `UnsupportedFieldAttributeWarning` for `validation_alias` on request models.
  - Root causes:
    - Missing `numpy` import in `speech_service.py` while new stream conversion code uses `np.ndarray` checks.
    - WebSocket handler attempted `send_json` after client already disconnected.
    - `validation_alias` metadata shape in models triggered warnings under current pydantic/python runtime.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Added `import numpy as np`.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added `send_ws_json()` safe sender helper in `/speech/transcribe/ws`.
      - Replaced direct `websocket.send_json(...)` calls with safe sender to avoid send-after-close crashes.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/models.py`
      - Refactored alias fields using `Annotated[...]` type aliases for request DTOs:
        - `TTSConfigRequest`
        - `SpeechSynthesisRequest`
      - Keeps compatibility for both `vieneu_*` and `tts_vieneu_*` payload keys while reducing schema warnings.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall` passed for updated backend files.
    - Runtime endpoint verification could not complete in this run because local AI backend listener was not reachable at probe time.
  - Remaining risk:
    - If backend process is down or stale, UI still appears as "mic recognized in browser but robot not hearing" due transport not connected; must ensure `dev:ai:bridge` instance is running healthy.

- Enhancement round 113 completed (VieNeu stream + websocket stability for realtime voice):
  - Fixed critical crash in VieNeu streaming path by ensuring NumPy is available in speech service runtime (`import numpy as np` in `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`).
  - Hardened websocket `/speech/transcribe/ws` final-send path in `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`:
    - when socket is closed, stop sending immediately and return early.
    - prevents repeated `Cannot call "send" once a close message has been sent.` cascades.
  - Normalized TTS request schemas in `services/ai-backend/app/models.py`:
    - removed alias-type indirection and attached `validation_alias` directly on model fields.

  - Additional stability patch:
    - `POST /sessions/{session_id}/turn/stream` now handles `httpx`/provider failures inside generator and emits NDJSON error chunk instead of crashing ASGI stream.

  - Enhancement round 115 completed (STT not triggering despite mic permission):
    - Root cause 1: order-mode acceptance logic was too strict, causing conversational phrases to be rejected as retry.

        - keep actionable check,
        - add conversational keyword acceptance,
        - reject very short/noise tokens only.

        - added force-finalize timer (`BACKEND_STT_FORCE_FINALIZE_MS=3600`),

        - clears force timer on final/stop/start transitions.

- Enhancement round 130 completed (VieNeu realtime research + player bug fix):
  - User request:
    - Keep VieNeu voice quality and enable true realtime smooth speech (no word-by-word pauses).
  - Internet research summary:
    - Reviewed VieNeu-TTS repo docs and streaming demo implementation.
    - Key finding: VieNeu realtime demo streams WAV header then PCM chunks and plays with AudioContext scheduling, not per-chunk <audio> elements.
  - Root cause in project:
    - Kiosk player treated WAV chunks as separate audio files (new Audio/Blob per chunk), introducing audible gaps and fragmented speech.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added `playVieneuWavStream()` using AudioContext + PCM scheduling for continuous playback.
      - Added WAV sample-rate parsing and repeated-header stripping logic for backend compatibility.
      - Updated `playBotSpeech()` engine routing:
        - if VieNeu requested/selected -> use VieNeu realtime stream path.
        - else keep fast edge blob fallback path.
      - Kept abort handling and UI face-state transitions consistent.
  - Validation:
    - `npm run build:ui` passed.
  - Impact:
    - VieNeu realtime now follows the same playback model as upstream demo behavior, removing chunk boundary pauses that sounded like one-word speech.

      - Added runtime prewarm (`prewarmVoiceRuntime`) called on kiosk init to warm AI URL probe and audio context unlock hooks.
      - Added autoplay detection (`isAutoplayBlockedError`) and browser TTS fallback helper (`speakWithBrowserFallback`).
      - Updated `playVieneuWavStream` to resume suspended `AudioContext` before scheduling PCM chunks.
      - Updated `playBotSpeech` fallback behavior: if stream/blob playback is blocked, fallback to browser speech instead of silent failure.

        - try backend session greeting first,

        - keep status in ready/listening state instead of hard error.

  - Expected impact:
    - On presence enter, robot should greet immediately more consistently.
    - Auto-greeting no longer gets stuck in hard-fail status when backend startup is slow.
    - Better first-audio reliability on kiosk browsers with autoplay restrictions.

- Debug round 132 completed (auto-greeting root cause fix, removed browser voice fallback):
  - Symptom:
    - Presence detected but greeting often failed early with status `Khong tao duoc loi chao tu dong.`
    - Browser fallback voice was used in some failures and sounded unnatural for Vietnamese.
  - Evidence collected:
    - Runtime `/health` showed AI backend healthy with `tts_engine=vieneu` and `vieneu_installed=true`.
    - `/sessions/start` can fail if core backend is unavailable because greeting build path still fetched menu.
    - Existing kiosk logic set cooldown timestamp before greeting success, so a first failed attempt delayed immediate retry.
  - Root cause:
    1) Backend `start_session()` indirectly depended on `core_client.list_menu()` via `_build_response()`, which is unnecessary for an empty-cart greeting and causes startup-time greeting failure.
    2) UI auto-greeting cooldown and retry behavior were not robust for backend cold-start races.
    3) Browser `speechSynthesis` fallback masked root cause and produced poor Vietnamese voice quality.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - `start_session()` now calls `_build_response(..., menu=[])`.
      - `_build_response()` now fetches menu only when `menu is None` (not for explicit empty list).
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added `test_start_session_does_not_require_core_menu` to prevent regression.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Removed browser speech fallback flow (no `speechSynthesis` fallback playback).
      - Added auto-greeting retry scheduler with bounded retries/backoff.
      - Moved cooldown update to success path only (`lastAutoGreetingAt` set after successful spoken greeting).
      - Kept audio/runtime prewarm and added VieNeu stream warmup call.
      - On autoplay-blocked errors, status now shows clear unblock instruction instead of fallback voice.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` passed (34 passed).
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Remaining risks:
    - If browser autoplay policy blocks audio output before any user interaction, speech still cannot start; UI now reports explicit unblock message instead of switching to low-quality fallback voice.

- Debug round 138 completed (VieNeu stream stutter root-cause + fixes):
  - Symptom:
    - VieNeu speech still sounded cut/choppy even when chat text was correct.
  - Evidence:
    - Stream probe on `/speech/synthesize/stream` showed repeated `RIFF` per chunk with chunk cadence around 1.3-1.7s for ~0.5s audio payload.
    - Direct SDK probe showed CPU `infer_stream` throughput below realtime; high playback rate amplified underruns.
  - Root causes:
    1) Backend stream path wrapped numpy chunks into full WAV every chunk (repeated header), not matching VieNeu realtime pattern.
    2) No active preempt signal for stale VieNeu stream jobs, so newer requests could wait behind old stream work.
    3) Kiosk default stream playback rate (`1.08`) was too aggressive for current CPU throughput.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Emit WAV header once + PCM16 chunk payload for ndarray stream chunks.
      - Add VieNeu stream preempt/cancel guard (new stream cancels previous active stream worker).
      - Add stream diagnostics (`audio_sec`, `realtime_factor`) and expose factor in `/speech/vieneu/diag`.
      - Add runtime stream tuning apply (`frames_per_chunk`, `lookforward`, `lookback`, `overlap`).
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added env settings:
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_FRAMES_PER_CHUNK`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_LOOKFORWARD`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_LOOKBACK`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_STREAM_OVERLAP_FRAMES`
    - `services/ai-backend/app/models.py`
      - Extended `TTSConfigRequest` with stream tuning fields + legacy aliases.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - `/health` and `/config/tts` now include VieNeu stream tuning fields.
      - `/speech/synthesize/stream` returns `audio/wav` when engine is explicitly VieNeu.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Set default `TTS_STREAM_PLAYBACK_RATE` to `1.0` (clamp `0.75-1.1`).
      - Add small prebuffer (2 chunks) before playback to reduce immediate underrun artifacts.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Added admin env controls for VieNeu stream tuning.
      - Updated preset defaults with safer playback rate `1.0`.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 34 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - CPU-only VieNeu stream can still run below realtime on long sentences; use `realtime_factor` logs to tune or move to faster backend mode.

- Enhance round 139 completed (VieNeu multi-mode support + anti-stutter runtime strategy):
  - User pain:
    - VieNeu still stuttered despite prior stream-format fixes; user expected realtime capability from official docs.
  - Additional findings:
    - Current stack always initialized VieNeu factory without mode/device controls, effectively locking runtime to default standard/cpu behavior.
    - Official VieNeu supports multiple inference modes (`standard`, `fast/gpu`, `xpu`, `remote`) and realtime claims are mainly aligned with fast/GPU paths.
    - On current CPU standard mode, measured stream throughput remained below realtime, which can cause audible underrun/stutter during live stream playback.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added VieNeu runtime fields:
        - `TTS_VIENEU_MODE`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_BACKBONE_DEVICE`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_CODEC_REPO`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_CODEC_DEVICE`
        - `TTS_VIENEU_REMOTE_API_BASE`
    - `services/ai-backend/app/models.py`
      - Extended `TTSConfigRequest` with matching fields + legacy aliases.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - `/health` now exposes VieNeu mode/device fields and `vieneu_stream_realtime_factor`.
      - `/config/tts` now updates/returns VieNeu mode/device settings and resets runtime when changed.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - VieNeu init now respects configured mode/device/remote settings:
        - `Vieneu(mode=<configured_mode>, **kwargs)`
      - Added mode-aware init attempts and logging (`vieneu_init_ok/failed` include mode).
      - Diagnostics now include mode/device/remote config for faster triage.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Added admin env controls for VieNeu mode/device/remote fields.
      - Updated realtime profiles:
        - CPU profile -> `standard/cpu`
        - GPU profiles -> `fast/cuda`
      - `/config/tts` payload now sends the new mode/device fields.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added `isVieneuRealtimeCapable()` gate:
        - stream playback only when mode is `fast/xpu` or backend reports high realtime factor.
      - If not realtime-capable, keep VieNeu voice but switch to full synth playback path (smooth speech, no word-by-word jitter).
      - Stream prewarm now only runs for `fast/xpu` mode.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall ...` passed for updated backend files.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 34 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Remaining note:
    - To get true low-latency realtime streaming, runtime should use VieNeu fast-capable backend (`TTS_VIENEU_MODE=fast`) with compatible GPU stack.

- Enhance round 142 completed (reduce TTS start delay after text appears):
  - User pain:
    - Voice starts 2-3s after text is already visible in chat.

    1) UI kept waiting for trailing stream chunks after final text had arrived.
    2) Realtime WS TTS flag defaulted off in template/runtime for some sessions.
    3) VieNeu realtime path often synthesized long full text at once, delaying first audible chunk.

      - In `/turn/stream` handler callback, stop stream immediately on `text_final` (`return false`) so TTS starts earlier.
      - Relaxed realtime gate: `allowRealtimeVieneuStream = forcedVieneu && (voiceTtsWsRealtimeEnabled || isVieneuRealtimeCapable())`.
      - Prewarm VieNeu stream when WS realtime flag is enabled, even outside fast/xpu mode.
      - Improved fallback logging with failed segment index/count.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Set `VOICE_TTS_WS_REALTIME` default to `true` in env template.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 36 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - Lower gap between first visible text and first audible speech, especially on longer replies.
    - More sessions use WS realtime path by default without manual admin toggling.

- Enhance round 143 completed (two-tier routing + faster perceived TTS response):
  - User pain:
    - Voice flow still felt slow versus Grok-style interaction.
    - Bridge was still on critical path too often for easy queries.
    - Audible response could lag after text appears.
  - Backend fixes (`services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`):
    - Added practical two-tier routing helper `_should_use_bridge(...)`:
      - Fast-local for easy `recommendation/greeting/cart_follow_up/fallback` cases.
      - Bridge escalation only for hard/long/time-sensitive keywords (`hom nay`, `moi nhat`, `gia`, `so sanh`, `tai sao`, etc.).
    - Added quick reply cache (TTL + bounded size) for repeated conversational prompts.
    - Eliminated stream double-bridge behavior:
      - `handle_turn_stream(...)` now marks turn as local-seed first, then streams bridge only when router says needed.
      - Added `bridge_stream_skipped` log with route reason.
    - Added route observability:
      - `reply_source` now logged together with `route_reason`.
  - Frontend fixes (`apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`):
    - Improved WS realtime TTS latency perception:
      - smarter `splitTextForFastTts(...)` (sentence + clause + length-aware chunking),
      - cached filler prompts and delayed filler injection while waiting (can be interrupted when real answer starts).
    - Added WS TTS delay logs (`[voice-tts-ws]`) including first-audio timing.
    - Extended prompt audio preload/cleanup to include both greeting and filler caches.
  - Tests/validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 38 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
    - Added/updated tests:
      - stream path uses bridge for hard query and avoids extra blocking `compose_reply` call,
      - fast recommendation path skips bridge for simple query.
  - Tradeoffs:
    - Hard-query detection is heuristic/rule-based and may need threshold tuning from real logs.
    - Filler audio improves perceived speed but can briefly play before the final answer starts in slower turns.
  - Remaining tech debt:
    - Add admin-exposed router thresholds for live tuning (keyword/length/confidence) without code changes.
    - Consider progressive TTS from early text deltas for true "speak-before-final" behavior in future round.

- Enhance round 144 completed (additional latency cut: early speak from stream + stricter bridge escalation):
  - User request:
    - Continue optimizing because perceived speed was still behind Grok-like instant response.
  - Backend optimization (`services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`):
    - Tightened bridge escalation thresholds to keep more turns on fast local path:
      - `BRIDGE_LONG_QUERY_WORDS_THRESHOLD: 20` (was 16)
      - `BRIDGE_LONG_QUERY_CHARS_THRESHOLD: 120` (was 90)
      - Removed question-mark-only escalation condition.
    - Result: fewer unnecessary bridge calls for medium short conversational turns.
  - Frontend optimization (`apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`):
    - Added progressive speech strategy for stream text:
      - New helpers: `extractEarlySpeakableText(...)`, `removeSpokenPrefixText(...)`.
      - Bot can start speaking a stable lead segment (ending at punctuation) before full final text arrives.
      - On final text, only speaks the remaining tail to avoid repeating the full sentence.
    - Improved UX masking while waiting:
      - filler prompt timer retained and auto-canceled when early speech starts.
      - if filler is already playing, it is interrupted cleanly before real answer speech.
    - Added minimum lead threshold `STREAM_EARLY_SPEECH_MIN_CHARS=42` to avoid reading too-short fragments.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q` -> 38 passed.
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py -q` -> 22 passed.
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` -> passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - Lower delay from first visible text to first meaningful speech.
    - Less dependence on bridge latency for everyday short queries.
  - Remaining tuning ideas:
    - Expose early-speech threshold and bridge escalation thresholds in Admin for live tuning.
    - Add shared persistent AudioContext for WS TTS path to cut per-call setup overhead further.

- Debug round 113 completed (partial STT decode error in streaming WebM):
  - Symptom:
    - Partial STT spammed `av.error.InvalidDataError` while processing `speech.webm`.
  - Root cause:
    - Partial audio snapshots can be incomplete WebM chunks; decoder may fail transiently before enough bytes arrive.
  - Fix applied:
    - In `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`, `_transcribe_partial_sync` now catches decode-only partial errors and returns empty transcript.
    - Added `_is_partial_decode_error` helper to classify known PyAV/FFmpeg decode failures.
    - Final/full transcription path is unchanged.
  - Verification:
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py` passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - Truly malformed stream packets still result in no partial text until final decode attempt.

- Debug round 145 completed (partial STT PyAV tuple-index crash in streaming):
  - Symptom:
    - Partial STT sometimes crashed with `IndexError: tuple index out of range` from `av.container.streams.StreamContainer.get` while decoding streaming snapshots.
  - Root cause:
    - Existing partial decode guard handled known FFmpeg/PyAV invalid-data EOF signatures, but did not classify this PyAV tuple-index variant seen on incomplete WebM partial chunks.
  - Fix applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Extended `_is_partial_decode_error` to detect this variant via:
        - message marker `tuple index out of range`
        - traceback markers under decode stack (`faster_whisper/audio.py`, `av/container/input.py`, `av/container/streams.py`) for `IndexError`.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py`
      - Added regression tests for decode-like `IndexError` classification and non-decode `IndexError` passthrough.
  - Verification:
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py services/ai-backend/tests/test_speech_service.py` passed.
    - Full pytest run in current shell failed at collection due missing local dependency `edge_tts`.
  - Remaining risk:
    - If PyAV introduces another novel decode signature, markers may need future extension; final/full STT flow remains unchanged.

- Enhance round 146 completed (bridge sentence-streaming + keepalive + SSE stream endpoint):
  - User goal:
    - Reduce first-audio latency by speaking sentence-by-sentence while bridge is still generating.
    - Eliminate bridge cold-start delay from idle periods.
  - Improvements applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/provider_client.py`
      - Upgraded `compose_reply_stream(...)` to accumulate token deltas and emit sentence-complete chunks on punctuation (`. ! ? 。 ！ ？ \n`) instead of tiny token fragments.
      - Added stream helpers `append_stream_content(...)` and `split_completed_sentences(...)`.
      - Added `ping(...)` method with `/ping` -> `/health` fallback for keepalive probes.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Added bridge keepalive settings:
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_ENABLED` (default true)
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_INTERVAL_SECONDS` (default 90)
        - `BRIDGE_KEEPALIVE_TIMEOUT_SECONDS` (default 5)
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added startup background keepalive task `_bridge_keepalive_loop()` and clean cancellation on shutdown.
      - `/health` now exposes keepalive runtime settings.
      - Added SSE endpoint `GET /chat/stream?session_id=...&text=...` returning `data: {"sentence": "..."}` chunks and `[DONE]` sentinel.
    - `scripts/bridge-server.mjs`
      - Added `GET /ping` lightweight 200 OK endpoint for low-cost keepalive.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added static keyword fast-cache path for short common utterances (greeting/menu/confirm) to return immediate local response without bridge roundtrip where applicable.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q -k "not trio"` -> 25 passed, 16 deselected.
    - `python -m py_compile` for updated backend modules -> passed.
    - Note: full anyio matrix still requires local `trio` package in this shell.
  - Tradeoffs / risks:
    - Sentence-gated stream may defer output for very long punctuation-less replies; final tail still flushes at end.
    - Static keyword cache is limited to short queries to avoid over-matching.
  - Frontend streaming TTS update:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html` now queues and plays incremental sentence segments during text stream (`earlySpeechQueuePromise`) instead of speaking only one early prefix then waiting for final tail.
    - Result: speech can continue sentence-by-sentence while bridge still generating next content.

- Enhance round 147 completed (bridge routing for non-ordering speech + anti-false-recommendation):
  - User pain point:
    - Non-ordering utterances (`tao ten la danh`, profanity, random chitchat) were incorrectly mapped to `recommendation` and returned static local menu suggestions.
    - Bridge stream was skipped for these turns, causing bot to feel "khong hieu" and repetitive.
  - Root causes:
    - Fallback recommendation path accepted any positive rank score, even weak token overlap.
    - `_rank_items` accepted short noise tokens, increasing accidental score.
    - `_should_use_bridge` defaulted to local template for most `fallback` and contextual `greeting` turns.
  - Fix applied:
    - Tightened recommendation gating:
      - Require top rank score >= `_MIN_RANK_SCORE_FOR_RECOMMENDATION` in both recommend-keyword branch and generic rank fallback.
      - Generic rank fallback now only applies when `has_ordering_hint` is true.
    - Reduced noisy token scoring in `_rank_items` by skipping tokens with length <= 2.
    - Improved bridge routing:
      - `fallback` now routes to bridge for profanity/chitchat/meaningful short context (>=2 tokens), local only for tiny noise.
      - `greeting` now routes simple greetings locally, but contextual greeting/chitchat to bridge.
    - Added helpers:
      - `_contains_profanity_text`
      - `_is_simple_greeting_text`
    - Refined `_is_chitchat` short-text heuristic from <=3 chars to <=2 chars.
  - Tests added:
    - `test_handle_turn_stream_routes_self_intro_to_greeting_bridge_scene`
    - `test_handle_turn_stream_routes_profanity_to_bridge_fallback_scene`
    - `test_non_ordering_chat_does_not_fall_into_recommendation_scene`
  - Validation:
    - `pytest services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -q -k "not trio"` -> 28 passed, 19 deselected.
    - `python -m py_compile services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py` passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Bridge traffic increases on contextual fallback/greeting turns; improves conversational correctness but may add small inference cost.

- Debug round 377 completed (VieNeu v2 Turbo GGUF overflow + wrong mode routing):
  - Symptom:
    - Repeated `502` on `/speech/synthesize` and stream path with error `Requested tokens (...) exceed context window of 2048`.
    - Runtime log still showed preset warning for `Doan` and behavior inconsistent with provider app.

    - Backend was initializing `pnnbao-ump/VieNeu-TTS-v2-Turbo-GGUF` using `mode=standard` (legacy path) instead of `mode=turbo`.
    - In installed `vieneu` SDK, `standard` path keeps `max_context=2048`; Turbo path uses 4096 and Turbo prompting.
    - Voice payload for turbo runtime needed `ref_codes`, while backend primarily populated `voice`.

    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py`
      - Added `_normalize_vieneu_mode(...)` with support for `turbo` / `turbo_gpu`.
      - Auto-switches runtime mode to `turbo` (or `turbo_gpu` on CUDA) when model path is v2 Turbo GGUF.
      - Added turbo init kwargs path (`backbone_repo` + `device`).
      - For turbo model, ignores custom `codec_repo` and uses SDK defaults.
      - Turbo voice selection now passes preset via `ref_codes` (instead of only `voice`).
    - `services/ai-backend/app/config.py`
      - Default `TTS_VIENEU_MODE` switched from `standard` to `turbo`.
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Runtime config API now accepts `turbo` and `turbo_gpu`.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Admin defaults/profile updated to `turbo` for CPU realtime v2 Turbo GGUF.
      - CPU ONNX readiness card accepts turbo CPU profile as valid.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Warmup gate now allows `turbo` / `turbo_gpu`.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/config.py services/ai-backend/app/main.py services/ai-backend/app/services/speech_service.py` passed.

- Enhance round 382 completed (stabilize VN intent parsing + STT alias robustness in conversation engine):
  - User pain point:
    - Chat flow unstable for STT-misheard commands like `gui di/gui y di`, and some order utterances failed to add items (e.g. `capuchino`).
    - Recommendation requests could fall through to weak fallback responses instead of clear menu suggestions.
  - Root causes:
    - `normalize_text(...)` dropped Vietnamese `d-with-stroke`, degrading intent words (`dat`, `di`, `goi y`).
    - Early `handle_turn(...)` intent checks ran before STT alias correction.
    - Recommendation branch required high rank threshold and skipped useful suggestions for short generic queries.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Preserve Vietnamese `d-with-stroke` as `d` during normalization.
      - Added aliases: `gui di`, `gui y di`, `gui y`, `gui i`, `goi i`, and `capuchino/capuccino/...` -> `cappuccino`.
      - Apply STT alias correction at start of `handle_turn(...)` so early intent routing uses corrected text.
      - Recommendation-intent path now always returns actionable suggestions even when rank score is weak.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added regressions for normalize (`Dat di`), `gui di` recommendation route, and `capuchino` -> `Cappuccino` add flow.
  - Validation:
    - Ran targeted pytest nodes on asyncio backend: 5 passed.
  - Tradeoff:
    - Alias mapping remains rule-based; uncommon STT mistakes may still require future alias expansion.

- Debug/Enhance round 388 completed (STT finalize hang fix: speaks done but no reply):
  - User pain point:
    - After user finished speaking, kiosk kept listening/waiting and did not respond.
  - Root cause:
    - Backend STT finalize timer was effectively reset by continuous recorder chunks, causing missed/late finalize in some sessions.
    - `voiceBackendFinalizing` could become stale true if backend failed to return `final`, blocking future finalize attempts.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Reworked `scheduleBackendFinalize()` into silence-aware checker:
        - no continuous reset storm,
        - finalize based on elapsed silence (`lastSpeechActivityAt`) rather than chunk cadence.
      - Added stuck-state recovery with `voiceBackendFinalizeIssuedAt`:
        - if finalize command is stale too long, auto-unblock and retry.
      - Updated force-finalize path with same stale recovery guard.
      - Reset finalize-issued timestamp on `final`, `onclose`, stop/start listening.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - User finishes speaking -> system finalizes and replies reliably instead of waiting indefinitely.

- Debug round 389 completed (browser interim submit timer no longer starves on repeated same transcript):
  - User pain point:
    - Voice UI still stuck in `Dang nghe: ...` after user stopped speaking, no response triggered.
  - Root cause:
    - Browser SpeechRecognition emitted identical interim text repeatedly; `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit(...)` reset timer every event, so `SUBMIT_SILENCE_MS` callback could be starved indefinitely.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added guard: if interim text is unchanged and submit timer already running, do not reset timer.
      - Improved timer state cleanup for pending interim timestamp bookkeeping.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - For repeated identical interim outputs (e.g., `mot ca phe muoi`), submit timer now fires and enqueues turn reliably.

- Debug round 390 completed (browser STT still waiting after speech stop - robust silence-submit):
  - Symptom:
    - UI stayed at `Dang nghe: ...` and did not submit/respond after user finished speaking.
  - Root cause:
    - Browser interim submit path used debounce-like timeout reset behavior; small interim variations could keep postponing submit.
    - `lastSpeechActivityAt` was refreshed too eagerly on repeated interim content.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Reworked `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit(...)` into silence-aware checker (similar principle as backend finalize).
      - Timer now persists and re-checks elapsed silence instead of full reset cycles on interim updates.
      - Added forced-submit upper bound (`max(1800, submitSilenceMs * 8)`) to prevent indefinite wait.
      - Updated browser `onresult` to call `markSpeechActivity()` only when interim content changed meaningfully.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Expected impact:
    - After user stops speaking, interim text should submit and trigger reply reliably (no endless waiting state).
- Debug round 391 completed (voice panel stuck on old interim text + next utterance dropped while robot busy):
  - Symptom:
    - Voice mini panel kept showing old `Dang nghe: ...` text.
    - User spoke next sentence while robot was replying, but system appeared to wait/treo and did not process follow-up reliably.
  - Evidence:
    - In `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit`, branch `if (isConversationTurnBusy())` cleared `voiceBrowserPendingInterim` immediately, causing data loss.
    - In `enqueueUserTurn`, `browser-interim` source was hard-dropped while busy.
  - Root cause:
    - Interim transcript pipeline dropped valid utterances during busy window instead of deferring submit.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit`: when busy, keep pending interim and reschedule check instead of clearing it.
      - Added status while waiting (`Robot dang phan hoi, da ghi nhan cau tiep theo...`) and status on submit (`Dang gui len backend...`) to avoid stale `Dang nghe: ...` feeling.
      - `enqueueUserTurn`: removed hard drop for `browser-interim` while busy; excluded `browser-interim` from rapid busy auto-drop filter.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
  - Remaining risk:
    - If user speaks many follow-ups during one long bot response, current design still keeps only latest pending interim (intended to avoid queue spam).
- Debug round 392 completed (voice status blinking + perceived no-listen/no-reply after busy-wait patch):
  - Symptom:
    - Voice status text flickered/chopped rapidly.
    - User felt robot was not listening/replying due unstable status updates.
  - Root cause:
    - Busy-wait loop in `scheduleBrowserInterimSubmit` updated status every retry tick (~100-220ms).
    - `setVoiceStatus` always rewrote DOM even when text/flag unchanged.
  - Fix applied:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Added status dedup cache (`voiceLastStatusText`, `voiceLastStatusThinking`) in `setVoiceStatus` to skip identical updates.
      - In browser interim busy branch, show busy notice only once per submit cycle (`busyNoticeShown`) instead of every timer tick.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

      - Reduced forced submit upper bound to `max(1200, submitSilenceMs * 2.5)` for faster handoff.

- Debug round 403 completed (Menu API external URL shows `Failed to fetch` in Admin/kiosk):
  - Symptom:
    - Admin service card for Menu API returned `Failed to fetch`.
    - Kiosk could not reliably load remote menu endpoint and could fall back to legacy local menu.
  - Evidence:
    - Remote endpoint `http://cnxvn.ddns.net:8080/...` responded `200` and JSON payload.
    - Response headers had no `Access-Control-Allow-Origin`, causing browser CORS failure.
    - Payload shape is `data.content[]` (not legacy `items[]`).
  - Root cause:
    - Frontend fetched remote menu directly from browser (CORS-blocked).
    - Menu health check in Admin also fetched remote URL directly.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/core-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added `GET /menu/proxy?source=...` server-side fetch + payload normalization.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/config.ts`
      - Added `resolveBrowserSafeMenuApiUrl(...)` and auto-proxy in `getMenuApiUrl()`.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Menu health check now uses browser-safe resolved URL.
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - Menu URL candidate now rewrites external URLs to core proxy.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
    - Core-backend pytest could not run in this shell (missing `fastapi` package in current env).

- Enhance round 171 completed (Admin-configurable tax with immediate kiosk sync):

- Debug round 172 completed (turn stream crash on Unicode surrogate in bridge text):
  - Symptom:
    - `/sessions/{id}/turn/stream` intermittently crashed with `UnicodeEncodeError: 'utf-8' codec can't encode character '\ud83d' ... surrogates not allowed`.
  - Evidence:
    - Stacktrace pointed to `services/ai-backend/app/main.py` in `response_stream` at NDJSON emit (`json.dumps(...).encode('utf-8')`).
    - Crash happened after bridge response, indicating malformed surrogate text in streamed payload.
  - Root cause:
    - Stream serialization assumed all payload strings are valid UTF-8 encodable Unicode; bridge output occasionally contains isolated surrogate code points.
  - Fix applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/main.py`
      - Added `_safe_json_text`, `_safe_sse_data`, `_safe_ndjson_line` helpers that serialize JSON then sanitize invalid surrogates via UTF-8 `errors='replace'` before emitting.
      - Replaced raw `json.dumps(...).encode('utf-8')` in both SSE `/chat/stream` and NDJSON `/sessions/{id}/turn/stream` paths with safe helpers.
  - Validation:
    - `python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/main.py` passed.
  - Remaining note:
    - `Execution context was destroyed, most likely because of a navigation` from bridge provider is separate (provider/browser context lifecycle) and now no longer crashes turn streaming due encoding.
- Enhance round 173 completed (Listen Mode applies instantly from Admin UI):
  - Symptom:
    - Operator changed Listen Mode in Voice panel but kiosk still behaved as continuous listening.
  - Root cause:
    - Listen Mode dropdown only updated local React form state; it did not immediately persist admin env config/sync event unless user performed separate save action.
  - Fix:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/src/AdminPage.tsx`
      - Added `applyVoiceListenModeInstant(...)` to update `VOICE_LISTEN_MODE` + `VOICE_ALWAYS_LISTEN`, persist via `saveAdminEnvConfig(...)`, refresh sync timestamp, and show notice.
      - Wired both Listen Mode dropdowns (voice panel + env field renderer) to use instant-apply handler.
  - Result:
    - Switching listen mode now propagates to kiosk immediately without extra save step.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.
- Enhance round 174 completed (conversation flow optimization for short replies and STT size mishearing):
  - User pain point:
    - Bot conversation was brittle in ordering flow:
      - `sai nhỏ` not reliably interpreted as size selection,
      - short negative reply `không` after add/size flow could drop to fallback,
      - bridge reply sometimes had broken Vietnamese spacing (`uố ng`, `muốnt hêm`, `tênm ón`).
  - Root causes:
    - Missing STT alias normalization for common `size` mishearing phrase variants.
    - No explicit handling for short negative replies when cart already exists.
    - Spacing repair was too generic and missed some high-frequency malformed phrase patterns.
  - Fixes applied:
    - `services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py`
      - Added STT aliases: `sai nho`/`sai vua`/`sai lon` -> `size ...`.
      - Added `SHORT_NEGATIVE_REPLY_KEYWORDS` + `_is_short_negative_reply_text(...)`.
      - In `handle_turn(...)`, when cart exists and user gives short negative reply:
        - if awaiting confirmation: switch to `cart_follow_up` (do not fallback), keep cart.
        - otherwise move to `ask_confirmation` with clear intent (`không thêm topping`, ask confirm).
      - Added targeted phrase repairs in `_repair_vietnamese_spacing_text(...)` for common corruptions:
        - `uố ng` -> `uống`,
        - `muốnt hêm` -> `muốn thêm`,
        - `tênm ón` -> `tên món`,
        - `khôngp hục`-like split -> `không phục`.
      - Extended broken-spacing protection scope to include recommendation scene checks.
    - `services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py`
      - Added regression tests:
        - recommendation reply spacing repair,
        - `sai nho` accepted as size alias,
        - short negative reply with existing cart routes to confirmation and keeps cart.
  - Validation:
    - `pytest -q services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -k "ensure_frontend_safe_reply_fallbacks_for_broken_recommendation_spacing"` passed.
    - `pytest -q services/ai-backend/tests/test_ai_backend.py -k "(conversation_engine_requires_size_before_adding_item or conversation_engine_accepts_sai_nho_as_size_alias or short_negative_reply_keeps_cart_and_moves_to_confirmation) and asyncio"` passed.
    - `python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py` passed.
  - Note:
    - `trio` parametrized test runs remain unavailable in this local environment (module not installed), same as previous rounds.
- Enhance round 175 completed (voice confirmation now opens order-review popup):
  - Symptom:
    - Button flow opened first confirmation popup, but voice flow only read back cart and did not show order review UI.
  - Root cause:
    - In kiosk voice pipeline (`processVoiceQueue`), after receiving backend scene `ask_confirmation`, frontend updated cart but never called `openOrderReview()`.
  - Fix:
    - `apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html`
      - In voice reply handling, when:
        - not manual turn,
        - not quick-checkout turn,
        - backend scene is `ask_confirmation`,
        - order not yet created,
        - cart has items,
        - review popup not already open,
      - then call `openOrderReview()` immediately.
  - Result:
    - Voice flow now matches button UX: first confirmation step pops up order review before final confirmation.
  - Validation:
    - `npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build` passed.

- Enhance round 179 completed (manual add cart overwrite fix, repro from Freeze Chocolate):
  - Root cause: during manual `+` add, optimistic local cart was later overwritten by `sessions/start` payload when it had no cart info or empty cart.
  - Fix: `startConversationSession(...)` now syncs cart only from normalized payload cart (`extractCartItemsFromPayload`).
  - Added guard for manual flow: if local cart already has items and startup cart is empty, preserve local cart (do not overwrite).
  - File touched: apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html
  - Validation: npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build passed.
- Enhance round 180 completed (Freeze Chocolate cart drop hardening):
  - Found additional overwrite path: manual turn stream/fallback payload with empty cart could still clear optimistic cart after `+` add.
  - Added `applyCartUpdateFromPayload(...)` guard to ignore empty cart payload on manual turns when local cart already has items.
  - Applied guard in all manual turn sync points: stream text_final, fallback turn response, and final payload reconciliation.
  - When payload cart update is rejected, flow now falls back to optimistic cart inference instead of clearing cart.
  - File touched: apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html
  - Validation: npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build passed.
- Enhance round 181 completed (Freeze Chocolate explicit-match fix):
  - Root cause identified: item-matching used only STT alias-corrected transcript; alias `chocolate -> socola` reduced confidence for exact item name `Freeze Chocolate`, causing `clarify_item` instead of auto-add.
  - Fix: `_match_explicit_items(...)` now evaluates both original normalized transcript and alias-corrected transcript for exact/token/fuzzy matching, taking the best signal.
  - Impact: exact English item names like `Freeze Chocolate` are no longer downgraded by alias replacement and should auto-add normally.
  - File touched: services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py
  - Validation: python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py passed.
  - Note: live API re-check was blocked at the moment by core connectivity error (`Khong the ket noi toi core backend`).
- Debug round 182 completed (Freeze Chocolate single-match still routed to clarify_item):
  - Symptom: utterances for Freeze Chocolate repeatedly returned `scene=clarify_item` with recommended_item_ids only `26` and empty cart.
  - Root cause: auto-add path required high confidence; when confidence dropped below threshold, even a single available match was sent to clarification.
  - Fix: in `available_matches` branch, enable auto-add when there is exactly one available match and transcript has ordering intent or explicit size hint.
  - File touched: services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py
  - Validation: python -m compileall services/ai-backend/app/services/conversation_engine.py passed.
  - Remaining risk: very noisy single-match utterances may auto-add more aggressively (acceptable for kiosk ordering UX).
- Enhance round 183 completed (prevent same-item different-size cart collapse in manual UI flow):
  - Symptom: adding same product with different sizes in kiosk UI could collapse/accumulate as one line after backend turn sync.
  - Root cause: manual turn payload cart from backend is item_id-based and could overwrite frontend optimistic cart that is size-key based.
  - Fix in frontend sync policy:
    - Ignore backend cart sync for manual turns (`applyCartUpdateFromPayload` returns false when `isManualTurn`).
    - Ignore `sessions/start` cart sync when source is manual.
    - Disable optimistic-reply fallback reconciliation for manual turns to avoid accidental merge.
  - Impact: manual add flow now preserves separate lines per size reliably in mini-cart/review popup.
  - File touched: apps/kiosk-ui/public/stitch_robot_3d_control_center.html
  - Validation: npm --prefix apps/kiosk-ui run build passed.
